By: guyc 04/Sep/12 11:30:47

Added some more points on the controller graph to cope with new rapid fire values in multiplayer.

GVR settings of 1, 2 and 3 are for the single player upgradable attachment.

New rates in the weapons spreadsheet can now be selectable via this gamevar in the following way:
GVR = 4 creates a 33% increase (Kriss goes from 18->24 bps, MP5A5 goes from 15 to 20 bps)
GVR = 5 creates a 37.5% increase (MP7 goes from 16 ->22 bps)
Scar uses the single player level 3 upgrade (25%) as it goes from 12 to 15 bps.
CBJ doubles its rate, and uses the GVR value of 6 to do this.

This is all specified in a column in guns.elx.

By: guyc 20/Aug/12 14:01:04

Plumbed in 2 more mixgroups.
MIX_SFX_CUT_SCENE_NO_SLOWMO
(does not have the time slowdown effect applied to it). Useful for doing "designed" slowdown effects during cutscenes (or anywhere else for that matter).

MIX_SFX_CUT_SCENE_TRUE_SLOWMO
This has a more mathematically correct pitch bend applied to it during slowdowns. Pitches down an octave at half game speed. Useful for correcting any lengthy cutscene sounds that span time slowdown moments.

By: guyc 24/May/12 10:23:03

Player weapon loop ending sound is now a standalone sfx triggered on each shot. A morph picks the indoor/outdoor sample via a sample-and-hold controller. This fixes the tiny glitches inbetween the loop and the ending that otherwise occur. It also provides us with the ability to resample and edit the different ending sounds.

This means that the predelay times within these sounds will have to match the length of one shot for that weapon. The idea is that the sound is fired off an each shot, but the sound is delayed by the duration of a shot with a culling setting of 1/steal.

By: guyc 18/May/12 11:11:18

Fixed one of the moonraker loader loops by duping samples within the loop. The problem lies with the mp3 encoder aligning the samples within the loop. Watch out for tonal samples with short loop points. Solution is to either

a) duplicate the loop data giving the encoder more of a chance to align it properly, or
b) set it to PCM/ADPCM

I've made a new ADPCM codec to do this.

By: guyc 06/Jan/12 13:30:47

Enemy M4 now uses stereo tail. Also, boosted source wav (needs doing in session file). Both overall volume and compression.

By: guyc 05/Jan/12 18:01:14

In a roundabout way, the distance to the RPG trail sounds sets the amount of bitcrushing on mixgroups.

The audible sounds (trail INNER and OUTER) send their distance to a gamevar. This gamevar is then used to drive the amount of bitcrushing via the MIXGROUP_FX controller.

When the trail disappears (i.e. the rocket explodes), a silent sound with no controller will stop. The release element of this sound resets the gamevar via a flat controller graph. As a safety measure, the gamevar is also reset via the RESET_MIXGROUPS event.

The overall effect is that the rocket is distorting groups of sounds around it.

By: guyc 05/Jan/12 17:30:11

Added a bitcrushing effect to mixgroup fx that activates via the Explosion_Close gamevar.

By: guyc 05/Jan/12 17:20:00

Added 4dB onto main_control_room wav and 5dB onto blast pit amb - not in the session though.
.

Prevented Speech group from getting stopped when LEVEL_COMPLETE event is triggered in single player. This will allow the mission fail speech to play in spec ops. The game now triggers the RESTART and QUIT events so speech is stopped when selecting these options. This will prevent in-game speech (e.g. barks) from playing once QUIT has been selected (because to quit, it has to return briefly to the game in the background). However, this will stop the "mission failed" speech (but you'd expect this to stop if you select 'quit' anyway).

By: steved 17/Jun/10 12:23:24

!!!! NOTE Speech will temporarily stop working with this publish !!!!

Rejig of Sound Bank layout to optimise Disc usage prior to receiving localistaion. TWO new sound bank slots are in: One is for all STREAMED speech (and can therefore be Generic) and the second is for INSTANT START streams. There is one bank per level for these, with 128k allocated. Needs setting up in a Spreadsheet when ChrisC has made available.

Generic speech bank is:

SB_SPEECH_GENERIC. This can be loaded on boot. The other banks should be referenced from leveldata spreadsheet.

By: guyc 04/Feb/10 11:53:16

Removed reverb from distant NPC gunfire sounds. A generic reverb type is applied in the batch process. For automatic weapons. the inner sound uses a shortened version of the player body, so reverb can be applied to this to artificially lengthen it in-game.

ALL automatic weapons now use an adapted version of the rapid-fire process. This is a little more channel hungry, but is more flexible in terms of culling and sample rates. It also means we can have uncompressed, PCM samples forming the start of each gun shot.
